                     */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum EngineError {\n    #[error(\"auction not found\")]\n      }\n    }\n\n    /// Convenience helper for tests/local dev.\n    pub fn with_memory_store(config: EngineConfig) -> Self {\n        Self::new(MemoryAuctionStore::default(), }\n\n    /* ----------------------------- API methods ----------------------------- */\n\n    /// Creates an auction and stores it. Emits `AuctionCreated`.\n    pub async fn create_auction(\n        &self,\n        params: CreateAuction,\n    ) -> Result<AuctionId, EngineError> {\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let auction = Auction {\n            id: AuctionId::new(),\n            nft_id: params.nft_id,\n            seller_id: params.seller_id,\n            reserve_price: params.reserve_price,\n            start_time: now,\n            end_time: now + params.duration,\n            status: AuctionStatus::Active,\n            highest_bid: None,\n        };\n        self.store.insert(auction.clone()).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionCreated(auction.id))?;\n        Ok(auction.id)\n    }\n\n    /// Places a new bid on an active auction.\n    pub async fn place_bid(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n        bidder_id: UserId,\n        amount: u128,\n    ) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if !auction.is_active(now) {\n            return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotActive);\n        }\n\n        if bidder_id == auction.seller_id {\n            return Err(EngineError::SellerCannotBid);\n        }\n\n        // First bid must be >= reserve.\n        if auction.highest_bid.is_none() && amount < auction.reserve_price {\n            return Err(EngineError::ReserveNotMet);\n        }\n\n        // Ensure minimum increment.\n        if let Some(ref high) = auction.highest_bid {\n            let min_required =\n                high.amount + Self::calc_increment(high.amount, self.min_increment_bps);\n            if amount < min_required {\n                return Err(EngineError::IncrementTooLow);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // TODO: anti-sniping extension window can be applied here.\n\n        auction.highest_bid = Some(Bid {\n            bidder_id,\n            amount,\n            timestamp: now,\n        });\n\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::BidPlaced {\n            auction_id,\n            bidder_id,\n            amount,\n        })?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Cancels an auction by its seller before any bids are placed.\n    pub async fn cancel_auction(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n        requester: UserId,\n    ) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if auction.seller_id != requester {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        if auction.highest_bid.is_some() || !matches!(auction.status, AuctionStatus::Active) {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        auction.status = AuctionStatus::Cancelled;\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionCancelled(auction_id))?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Finalize an auction that reached its end time. Returns the winner if any.\n    pub async fn finalize_auction(\n        &self,\n        auction_id: AuctionId,\n    ) -> Result<Option<(UserId, u128)>, EngineError> {\n        let mut auction = match self.store.get(auction_id).await? {\n            Some(a) => a,\n            None => return Err(EngineError::AuctionNotFound),\n        };\n\n        if !auction.should_finalize(Utc::now()) {\n            return Err(EngineError::InvalidAuctionState);\n        }\n\n        auction.status = AuctionStatus::Finalized;\n        let winner_info = auction\n            .highest_bid\n            .as_ref()\n            .map(|b| (b.bidder_id, b.amount));\n\n        self.store.update(&auction).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::AuctionFinalized {\n            auction_id,\n            winner: winner_info.map(|t| t.0),\n            amount: winner_info.map(|t| t.1),\n        })?;\n\n        // TODO: trigger settlement workflow (escrow smart contract, royalties, etc.)\n        Ok(winner_info)\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------- Internals ------------------------------ */\n\n    fn emit(&self, evt: AuctionEvent) -> Result<(), EngineError> {\n        self.event_tx\n            .send(evt)\n            .map_err(|_| EngineError::Broadcast)\n            .map(|_| ())\n    }\n\n    fn calc_increment(current: u128, bps: u16) -> u128 {\n        // basis points: 1 bps = 0.01 %\n        (current * bps as u128) / 10_000u128\n    }\n\n    /* ----------------------------- Finalize loop ---------------------------- */\n\n    /// Spawns a Tokio task that periodically finalizes elapsed auctions.\n    ///\n    /// NOTE: In a clustered deployment only the leader instance should run the\n    /// loop to avoid double-finalization.  This is achieved via distributed\n    /// locks (e.g. etcd/consul) at the service orchestrator layer.\n    pub fn spawn_finalize_loop(self, interval: StdDuration) -> JoinHandle<()> {\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let mut ticker = tokio::time::interval(interval);\n            loop {\n                ticker.tick().await;\n                let now = Utc::now();\n                match self.store.all_due_for_finalize(now).await {\n                    Ok(ids) => {\n                        for id in ids {\n                            // best effort, log errors\n                            if let Err(e) = self.finalize_auction(id).await {\n                                tracing::warn!(\n                                    auction_id = ?id,\n                                    error = ?e,\n                                    \"failed to finalize auction\"\n                                );\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => tracing::error!(error = ?e, \"finalize loop failed to fetch auctions\"),\n                }\n            }\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Engine configuration                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct EngineConfig {\n    pub min_increment_bps: u16,\n}\n\nimpl Default for EngineConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self { min_increment_bps: 50 } // 0.5%\n    }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                   Display                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nimpl fmt::Display for AuctionId {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        self.0.fmt(f)\n    }\n}\n```",

It supports multiple\n//! signing curves (Ed25519 and Secp256k1 today; BLS can be added behind a\n//! feature-flag) and uses Argon2 + ChaCha20-Poly1305 to protect keys at\n//! rest.\n//!\n//! The module follows a Strategy pattern where each curve implements the\n//! `SigningCurve` trait.  A very small, file\u2013based keystore is provided for\n//! demo/PoC purposes; in production an HSM or KMS implementation should\n//! instead be plugged in via the same trait.\n//!\n//!       // 2) Encrypt the secret key with Argon2 + ChaCha20-Poly1305\n        let (ciphertext, salt, nonce) = encrypt_secret(password, &sk)?;\n\n        // 3) Store on disk\n        let wallet =      .curves\n            .get(meta.algo)\n            .ok_or(KeyManagerError::UnsupportedAlgorithm)?;\n\n        let sk = decrypt_secret(\n            password,\n            &meta.encrypted_sk,\n }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Ed25519 &self,\n        public: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), KeyManagerError> {\n        use k256::ecdsa::{signature::Verifier as _, Signature, KeyStore: Send + Sync {\n    async fn put(&self, wallet: &WalletMeta) -> Result<(), KeyManagerError>;\n    async fn get(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<Option<WalletMeta>, KeyManagerError>;\n}\n\n/// A very small file-based keystore.\n///\n/// Thread-safe via `RwLock` plus atomic write-to-tmp-then-rename.\nstruct FileKeyStore {\n    path:   PathBuf,\n    cache:  RwLock<Vec<WalletMeta>>,\n}\n\nimpl FileKeyStore {\n    async fn open<P: AsRef<Path>>(p: P) -> Result<Self, KeyManagerError> {\n        let path = p.as_ref().to_path_buf();\n        if !path.exists() {\n            // create empty file\n            tokio::fs::write(&path, b\"[]\").await?;\n        }\n\n        let data = tokio::fs::read(&path).await?;\n        let wallets: Vec<WalletMeta> = serde_json::from_slice(&data)?;\n        Ok(Self {\n            path,\n            cache: RwLock::new(wallets),\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn persist(&self, list: &[WalletMeta]) -> Result<(), KeyManagerError> {\n        let tmp_path = self\n            .path\n            .with_extension(\"tmp\");\n\n        let data = serde_json::to_vec_pretty(list)?;\n        // atomic write to tmp then rename\n        tokio::task::spawn_blocking({\n            let tmp_path = tmp_path.clone();\n            let data = data.clone();\n            move || -> Result<(), KeyManagerError> {\n                let mut tmp_file = File::create(&tmp_path)?;\n                tmp_file.write_all(&data)?;\n                tmp_file.sync_all()?;\n                fs::rename(&tmp_path, &self.path)?;\n                Ok(())\n            }\n        })\n        .await??;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl KeyStore for FileKeyStore {\n    async fn put(&self, wallet: &WalletMeta) -> Result<(), KeyManagerError> This module owns the lifecycle of a governance proposal\u2014from\n//! creation to finalization\u2014inside the CanvasChain Symphony governance\n//! micro-service.  It is intentionally decoupled from concrete storage,\n//! crypto or transport layers via small, test-friendly traits so that\n//! the engine can be reused inside CLI tools, HTTP controllers or gRPC\n//! handlers without recompilation.\n\n#![allow(clippy::module_name_repetitions)]\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::{HashMap, HashSet},\n    sync::Arc,\n    time::Duration,\n};\n\nuse async_trait::async_trait;\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse log::{debug, error, info, warn};\nuse rand::Rng;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::{\n    sync::RwLock,\n    task::JoinHandle,\n    time::{self, Instant},\n};\nuse uuid::Uuid;\n\n/// Error type returned by the proposal engine.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ProposalError {\n    #[error(\"storage error: {0}\")]\n    Storage(String),\n    #[error(\"signature verification failed\")]\n    InvalidSignature,\n    #[error(\"proposal not found: {0}\")]\n    NotFound(Uuid),\n    #[error(\"vote already cast by voter\")]\n    DuplicateVote,\n    #[error(\"proposal already finalized\")]\n    Finalized,\n    #[error(\"internal error: {0}\")]\n    Internal(String),\n}\n\n/// Supported vote choices.\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum VoteChoice {\n    Yes,\n    No,\n    Abstain,\n}\n\n/// Current status of a proposal.\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum ProposalStatus {\n    Pending,\n    Active,\n    Finalized,\n}\n\n/// A governance proposal.  The semantics of the payload are opaque to\n/// the proposal engine and can encode anything from smart-contract\n/// upgrades to art-movement parameters.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Proposal {\n    pub id: Uuid,\n    pub author: String,\n    pub status: ProposalStatus,\n    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub expires_at: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub payload: serde_json::Value,\n    pub votes: HashMap<String, VoteChoice>,\n}\n\n/// Governance parameters under which a proposal is evaluated.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug)]\npub struct GovernanceParameters {\n    /// Minimum voting period.\n    pub voting_period: Duration,\n    /// Quorum required as percentage (0\u2013100).\n    pub quorum_pct: u8,\n    /// Minimum \u201cYes\u201d ratio required to pass (0\u2013100).\n    pub pass_threshold_pct: u8,\n}\n\n/// Event emitted by the proposal engine to the wider event-bus.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum GovernanceEvent {\n    ProposalCreated { proposal_id: Uuid, author: String },\n    VoteCast {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: String,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n    },\n    ProposalFinalized {\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        result: ProposalOutcome,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Finalization result.\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum ProposalOutcome {\n    Accepted,\n    Rejected,\n    QuorumNotMet,\n}\n\n/// Storage abstraction \u2013 can be backed by Postgres, RocksDB, Redis, etc.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait ProposalStore: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn save_proposal(&self, proposal: &Proposal) -> Result<(), ProposalError>;\n\n    async fn load_proposal(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<Proposal, ProposalError>;\n\n    async fn save_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError>;\n\n    async fn list_active(&self) -> Result<Vec<Proposal>, ProposalError>;\n\n    async fn finalize(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        outcome: ProposalOutcome,\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError>;\n}\n\n/// Event publisher abstraction \u2013 decouples the engine from concrete\n/// transport: NATS, Kafka, in-process channel, etc.\n#[async_trait]\npub trait EventPublisher: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn publish(&self, event: GovernanceEvent);\n}\n\n/// Signature verification strategy.  Each wallet/curve implementation\n/// can plug its own verifier (Ed25519, BLS, post-quantum\u2026).\n#[async_trait]\npub trait SignatureVerifier: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    async fn verify(\n        &self,\n        wallet_address: &str,\n        payload: &[u8],\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError>;\n}\n\n/// A default in-memory storage for local testing.\n///\n/// THIS IS NOT SUITABLE FOR PRODUCTION but helps keeping the code\n/// self-contained for demonstration purposes.\n#[derive(Default)]\npub struct InMemoryStore {\n    proposals: RwLock<HashMap<Uuid, Proposal>>,\n}\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl ProposalStore for InMemoryStore {\n    async fn save_proposal(&self, proposal: &Proposal) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        self.proposals\n            .write()\n            .await\n            .insert(proposal.id, proposal.clone());\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn load_proposal(&self, id: Uuid) -> Result<Proposal, ProposalError> {\n        self.proposals\n            .read()\n            .await\n            .get(&id)\n            .cloned()\n            .ok_or(ProposalError::NotFound(id))\n    }\n\n    async fn save_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let mut map = self.proposals.write().await;\n        let proposal = map\n            .get_mut(&proposal_id)\n            .ok_or(ProposalError::NotFound(proposal_id))?;\n\n        if proposal.status != ProposalStatus::Active {\n            return Err(ProposalError::Finalized);\n        }\n        if proposal.votes.contains_key(voter) {\n            return Err(ProposalError::DuplicateVote);\n        }\n\n        proposal.votes.insert(voter.to_owned(), choice);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn list_active(&self) -> Result<Vec<Proposal>, ProposalError> {\n        Ok(self\n            .proposals\n            .read()\n            .await\n            .values()\n            .filter(|p| p.status == ProposalStatus::Active)\n            .cloned()\n            .collect())\n    }\n\n    async fn finalize(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        _outcome: ProposalOutcome,\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let mut map = self.proposals.write().await;\n        let proposal = map\n            .get_mut(&proposal_id)\n            .ok_or(ProposalError::NotFound(proposal_id))?;\n        proposal.status = ProposalStatus::Finalized;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// A no-op event publisher, useful for CLI & tests.\npub struct NullPublisher;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl EventPublisher for NullPublisher {\n    async fn publish(&self, _event: GovernanceEvent) {\n        // swallow\n    }\n}\n\n/// The main fa\u00e7ade exposed to the outer world.  All methods are\n/// thread-safe and async aware.\npub struct ProposalEngine<S, E, V>\nwhere\n    S: ProposalStore,\n    E: EventPublisher,\n    V: SignatureVerifier,\n{\n    store: Arc<S>,\n    events: Arc<E>,\n    verifier: Arc<V>,\n    config: GovernanceParameters,\n    /// Task handle for the background finalizer loop.\n    finalizer_task: RwLock<Option<JoinHandle<()>>>,\n}\n\nimpl<S, E, V> ProposalEngine<S, E, V>\nwhere\n    S: ProposalStore,\n    E: EventPublisher,\n    V: SignatureVerifier,\n{\n    pub fn new(store: Arc<S>, events: Arc<E>, verifier: Arc<V>) -> Self {\n        let config = GovernanceParameters {\n            voting_period: Duration::from_secs(60 * 60 * 24), // 24h\n            quorum_pct: 15,\n            pass_threshold_pct: 50,\n        };\n\n        Self {\n            store,\n            events,\n            verifier,\n            config,\n            finalizer_task: RwLock::new(None),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Spawns the periodic finalization loop.  Calling this twice is a\n    /// no-op.\n    pub async fn start(&self) {\n        let mut guard = self.finalizer_task.write().await;\n        if guard.is_some() {\n            return;\n        }\n        let store = Arc::clone(&self.store);\n        let events = Arc::clone(&self.events);\n        let params = self.config.clone();\n\n        *guard = Some(tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let mut ticker = time::interval(Duration::from_secs(30));\n            loop {\n                ticker.tick().await;\n                if let Err(err) = finalize_expired(&store, &events, &params).await {\n                    error!(\"auto-finalization cycle failed: {err:?}\");\n                }\n            }\n        }));\n    }\n\n    /// Creates and stores a new proposal.  The caller is responsible for\n    /// signing the payload.\n    ///\n    /// `signature` must verify against `author` and the payload bytes\n    /// (as canonical JSON).\n    pub async fn create_proposal(\n        &self,\n        author: &str,\n        payload: serde_json::Value,\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Uuid, ProposalError> {\n        let json_bytes = serde_json::to_vec(&payload)\n            .map_err(|e| ProposalError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        self.verifier\n            .verify(author, &json_bytes, signature)\n            .await?;\n\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let expires_at = now + chrono::Duration::from_std(self.config.voting_period)\n            .map_err(|e| ProposalError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        let proposal = Proposal {\n            id: Uuid::new_v4(),\n            author: author.to_owned(),\n            status: ProposalStatus::Active,\n            created_at: now,\n            expires_at,\n            payload,\n            votes: HashMap::default(),\n        };\n\n        self.store.save_proposal(&proposal).await?;\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::ProposalCreated {\n                proposal_id: proposal.id,\n                author: author.to_owned(),\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(proposal.id)\n    }\n\n    /// Cast a vote on an active proposal.\n    pub async fn cast_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        // Message to sign = proposal_id (16 bytes) || choice (1 byte)\n        let mut msg = proposal_id.as_bytes().to_vec();\n        msg.push(choice as u8);\n\n        self.verifier.verify(voter, &msg, signature).await?;\n\n        self.store\n            .save_vote(proposal_id, voter, choice)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| {\n                debug!(\"save_vote failed: {e}\");\n                e\n            })?;\n\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::VoteCast {\n                proposal_id,\n                voter: voter.to_owned(),\n                choice,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Forces finalization of an active proposal, ignoring `expires_at`\n    /// (useful for emergency admin operations).\n    pub async fn finalize_now(&self, proposal_id: Uuid) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let proposal = self.store.load_proposal(proposal_id).await?;\n        let outcome = compute_outcome(&proposal, &self.config);\n        self.store.finalize(proposal_id, outcome).await?;\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::ProposalFinalized { proposal_id, result: outcome })\n            .await;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Computes the outcome according to yes/no/abstain counts and the\n/// engine\u2019s governance parameters.\nfn compute_outcome(proposal: &Proposal, params: &GovernanceParameters) -> ProposalOutcome {\n    let total_votes = proposal.votes.len() as u64;\n    if total_votes == 0 {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes = proposal\n        .votes\n        .values()\n        .filter(|&&c| c == VoteChoice::Yes)\n        .count() as u64;\n    let no = proposal\n        .votes\n        .values()\n        .filter(|&&c| c == VoteChoice::No)\n        .count() as u64;\n    let abstain = total_votes - yes - no;\n\n    debug!(\n        \"Computing outcome \u2013 yes:{yes}, no:{no}, abstain:{abstain}, total:{total_votes}\"\n    );\n\n    let quorum_met = (total_votes * 100 / u64::MAX.max(total_votes)) >= params.quorum_pct as u64;\n\n    if !quorum_met {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_pct = yes * 100 / total_votes;\n    if yes_pct >= params.pass_threshold_pct as u64 {\n        ProposalOutcome::Accepted\n    } else {\n        ProposalOutcome::Rejected\n    }\n}\n\n/// Periodic task for auto-finalizing expired proposals.\nasync fn finalize_expired<S: ProposalStore, E: EventPublisher>(\n    store: &Arc<S>,\n    events: &Arc<E>,\n    params: &GovernanceParameters,\n) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n    let now = Utc::now();\n    for mut proposal in store.list_active().await? {\n        if proposal.expires_at <= now {\n            let outcome = compute_outcome(&proposal, params);\n            store.finalize(proposal.id, outcome).await?;\n            events\n                .publish(GovernanceEvent::ProposalFinalized {\n                    proposal_id: proposal.id,\n                    result: outcome,\n                })\n                .await;\n            info!(\"proposal {} finalized with result {:?}\", proposal.id, outcome);\n        }\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// A mock signature verifier that accepts 1% of the messages randomly\n/// as invalid.  Replace with a real crypto verifier in production.\npub struct PseudoVerifier;\n\n#[async_trait]\nimpl SignatureVerifier for PseudoVerifier {\n    async fn verify(\n        &self,\n        _wallet_address: &str,\n        _payload: &[u8],\n        _signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        let mut rng = rand::thread_rng();\n        let rejected: bool = rng.gen_bool(0.01);\n        if rejected {\n            Err(ProposalError::InvalidSignature)\n        } else {\n            Ok(())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use serde_json::json;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn happy_path() {\n        let engine = ProposalEngine::new(\n            Arc::new(InMemoryStore::default()),\n            Arc::new(NullPublisher),\n            Arc::new(PseudoVerifier),\n        );\n\n        let payload = json!({\n            \"type\": \"change_quorum\",\n            \"new_quorum\": 20\n        });\n        let author = \"wallet_1\";\n\n        let proposal_id = engine\n            .create_proposal(author, payload, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"create proposal\");\n\n        engine\n            .cast_vote(proposal_id, \"voter_a\", VoteChoice::Yes, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"vote a\");\n\n        engine\n            .cast_vote(proposal_id, \"voter_b\", VoteChoice::Yes, &[0u8; 64])\n            .await\n            .expect(\"vote b\");\n\n        engine.finalize_now(proposal_id).await.expect(\"finalize\");\n\n        let proposal = engine\n            .store\n            .load_proposal(proposal_id)\n            .await\n            .expect(\"load final\");\n        assert_eq!(proposal.status, ProposalStatus::Finalized);\n    }\n}\n```",

    "content": "```rust\n//! Persistent world-state database abstraction for CanvasChain Symphony.\n//!\n//! The `StateDb` is the canonical source of truth for chain execution.  It\n//! stores **accounts**, **contract byte-code** and **key\u2013value storage** for\n//! every smart contract.  Each block commit generates a deterministic *state\n//! root* (a Blake3 Merkle accumulation of all key\u2013value pairs) that can later\n//! be proven against light-client requests or off-chain indexers.\n//!\n//! Elasticity requirements of the Symphony runtime dictate that the database\n//! must support:\n//!   * atomic multi-key updates (Write-Set)\n//!   * cheap, read-only snapshots per block height\n//!   * forward-only pruning (retain the last *N* roots and fast-prune the rest)\n//!\n//! This implementation relies on `sled` for embedded, high-performance storage\n//! and an append-only **versioned column family** layout to avoid write\n//! amplification while retaining historical states.\n\nuse std::{\n    path::{Path, PathBuf},\n    sync::{\n        atomic::{AtomicU64, Ordering},\n        Arc,\n    },\n};\n\nuse blake3::Hasher;\nuse parking_lot::RwLock;\nuse serde::{de::DeserializeOwned, Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse sled::{\n    transaction::{\n        ConflictableTransactionError, TransactionError, TransactionResult, Transactional,\n        TransactionalTree,\n    },\n    Db, IVec,\n};\nuse thiserror::Error;\nuse tokio::sync::broadcast;\n\n/// Logical identifier for an account or contract.\npub type Address = [u8; 32];\n\n/// Hashed representation of the entire world state for a given block height.\npub type StateRoot = [u8; 32];\n\n/// Ordering key prefix for versioned writes: `{height}/{raw_key}`.\n///\n/// We keep the numerical height in big-endian to preserve lexicographic order.\nfn compose_versioned_key(height: u64, raw_key: &[u8]) -> Vec<u8> {\n    let mut out = Vec::with_capacity(8 + raw_key.len());\n    out.extend_from_slice(&height.to_be_bytes());\n    out.extend_from_slice(raw_key);\n    out\n}\n\n/// Decode a versioned key returning `(height, raw_key)`.\nfn split_versioned_key(versioned: &[u8]) -> (u64, &[u8]) {\n    let (height_bytes, raw) = versioned.split_at(8);\n    (\n        u64::from_be_bytes(height_bytes.try_into().expect(\"8 bytes\")),\n        raw,\n    )\n}\n\n/// High-level account record stored in the `StateDb`.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub struct AccountState {\n    pub balance: u128,\n    pub nonce: u64,\n    /// Hash of contract bytecode (if any).\n    pub code_hash: Option<[u8; 32]>,\n    /// Merklized root of the contract storage tree.\n    pub storage_root: [u8; 32],\n}\n\nimpl Default for AccountState {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            balance: 0,\n            nonce: 0,\n            code_hash: None,\n            storage_root: [0u8; 32],\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Arbitrary write operation encoded in a block's *write-set*.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum WriteOp<V> {\n    Put(Vec<u8>, V),\n    Delete(Vec<u8>),\n}\n\n/// Aggregated writes performed by the execution engine for a single block.\npub type WriteSet<V> = Vec<WriteOp<V>>;\n\n/// Notification emitted after every successful `commit_block`.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct StateCommitEvent {\n    pub block_height: u64,\n    pub new_state_root: StateRoot,\n}\n\n/// Custom errors bubbled up by the `StateDb`.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum StateDbError {\n    #[error(\"sled error: {0}\")]\n    Sled(#[from] sled::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"serialization error: {0}\")]\n    Bincode(#[from] bincode::Error),\n\n    #[error(\"conflicting write transaction\")]\n    Conflict,\n\n    #[error(\"requested historical height ({requested}) is pruned \u2013 oldest available: {oldest}\")]\n    Pruned { requested: u64, oldest: u64 },\n}\n\n/// Primary database wrapper offering high-level typed APIs.\npub struct StateDb {\n    db: Db,\n    /// Tree for versioned state entries.\n    tree: sled::Tree,\n    /// Monotonically increasing block height.\n    current_height: AtomicU64,\n    /// Oldest height still retained (everything below is pruned).\n    oldest_height: AtomicU64,\n    /// Broadcast channel for commit notifications.\n    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<StateCommitEvent>,\n    /// Path on disk (used on `prune`).\n    _path: PathBuf,\n    /// Global rw-lock for snapshot safety.\n    guard: Arc<RwLock<()>>,\n}\n\nimpl StateDb {\n    /// Open or create a new `StateDb` at `path`.\n    pub fn open<P: AsRef<Path>>(path: P) -> Result<Self, StateDbError> {\n        let db = sled::open(&path)?;\n        let tree = db.open_tree(\"state\")?;\n\n        // Determine the current and oldest heights by scanning prefix keys.\n        let (mut current_height, mut oldest_height) = (0u64, u64::MAX);\n        for key in tree.iter().keys() {\n            let k = key?;\n            let (h, _) = split_versioned_key(&k);\n            if h > current_height {\n                current_height = h;\n            }\n            if h < oldest_height {\n                oldest_height = h;\n            }\n        }\n        if oldest_height == u64::MAX {\n            oldest_height = 0;\n        }\n\n        let (event_tx, _) = broadcast::channel(64);\n        Ok(Self {\n            db,\n            tree,\n            current_height: AtomicU64::new(current_height),\n            oldest_height: AtomicU64::new(oldest_height),\n            event_tx,\n            _path: path.as_ref().to_path_buf(),\n            guard: Arc::new(RwLock::new(())),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to state-commit events.\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<StateCommitEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n\n    /// Retrieve the value associated with `raw_key` *at the latest height*.\n    pub fn get<V: DeserializeOwned>(&self, raw_key: &[u8]) -> Result<Option<V>, StateDbError> {\n        let height = self.current_height.load(Ordering::SeqCst);\n        self.get_at(height, raw_key)\n    }\n\n    /// Retrieve a historical value at `height`.\n    pub fn get_at<V: DeserializeOwned>(\n        &self,\n        height: u64,\n        raw_key: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Option<V>, StateDbError> {\n        let oldest = self.oldest_height.load(Ordering::SeqCst);\n        if height < oldest {\n            return Err(StateDbError::Pruned {\n                requested: height,\n                oldest,\n            });\n        }\n\n        let _r = self.guard.read(); // protect against concurrent pruning\n        let versioned_key = compose_versioned_key(height, raw_key);\n        Ok(self\n            .tree\n            .get(versioned_key)?\n            .map(|ivec| bincode::deserialize(&ivec))\n            .transpose()?)\n    }\n\n    /// Store a single value at the *next* block height.\n    ///\n    /// This is mostly useful for tests; production execution typically uses\n    /// `commit_block` that atomically writes a full `WriteSet`.\n    pub fn put<V: Serialize>(&self, raw_key: &[u8], value: &V) -> Result<(), StateDbError> {\n        self.commit_block::<V>(WriteSet::from([WriteOp::Put(\n            raw_key.to_vec(),\n            value.clone(),\n        )]))\n        .map(|_| ())\n    }\n\n    /// Atomically apply a `write_set`, advance `current_height` and\n    /// deterministically compute the new `StateRoot`.\n    pub fn commit_block<V: Serialize>(&self, write_set: WriteSet<V>) -> Result<StateRoot, StateDbError> {\n        let new_height = self.current_height.load(Ordering::SeqCst) + 1;\n        {\n            // Acquire read-lock to forbid pruning during commit.\n            let _r = self.guard.read();\n            // --- transactional write ---\n            let result: TransactionResult<(), StateDbError, _> =\n                (&self.tree).transaction(|tx_tree| {\n                    for op in &write_set {\n                        match op {\n                            WriteOp::Put(k, v) => {\n                                let vk = compose_versioned_key(new_height, k);\n                                let bytes = bincode::serialize(v)?;\n                                tx_tree.insert(vk, bytes)\n                                    .map_err(|e| ConflictableTransactionError::Abort(StateDbError::Sled(e)))?;\n                            }\n                            WriteOp::Delete(k) => {\n                                let vk = compose_versioned_key(new_height, k);\n                                tx_tree.remove(vk)\n                                    .map_err(|e| ConflictableTransactionError::Abort(StateDbError::Sled(e)))?;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Ok(())\n                });\n\n            match result {\n                Ok(_) => {}\n                Err(TransactionError::Storage(e)) => return Err(StateDbError::Sled(e)),\n                Err(TransactionError::Abort(e)) => return Err(e),\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Sync to disk.\n        self.db.flush()?;\n\n        // Re-compute and persist new root.\n        let new_root = self.compute_state_root(new_height)?;\n        self.current_height.store(new_height, Ordering::SeqCst);\n\n        // Notify subscribers \u2013 ignore send failures (no active listeners).\n        let _ = self\n            .event_tx\n            .send(StateCommitEvent { block_height: new_height, new_state_root: new_root });\n\n        Ok(new_root)\n    }\n\n    /// Deterministically compute the Blake3 root for a given `height`.\n    ///\n    /// The root is the hash of the concatenation of `hash(key) || hash(value)`\n    /// in lexicographic key order.  While *not* a Patricia-Merkle tree, this\n    /// approach provides collision resistance and is fast to compute.\n    pub fn compute_state_root(&self, height: u64) -> Result<StateRoot, StateDbError> {\n        let prefix = height.to_be_bytes();\n        let mut hasher = Hasher::new();\n\n        for kv in self.tree.scan_prefix(prefix) {\n            let (k, v) = kv?;\n            hasher.update(blake3::hash(&k).as_bytes());\n            hasher.update(blake3::hash(&v).as_bytes());\n        }\n        Ok(*hasher.finalize().as_bytes())\n    }\n\n    /// Permanently remove historical states below `keep_from_height`.\n    pub fn prune(&self, keep_from_height: u64) -> Result<(), StateDbError> {\n        {\n            // Exclusive lock to block reads while we delete keys.\n            let _w = self.guard.write();\n            let oldest = self.oldest_height.load(Ordering::SeqCst);\n            if keep_from_height <= oldest {\n                // Nothing to do.\n                return Ok(());\n            }\n\n            // Delete per-key.\n            for kv in self.tree.range(..compose_versioned_key(keep_from_height, b\"\")) {\n                let (k, _) = kv?;\n                self.tree.remove(k)?;\n            }\n            self.db.flush()?;\n            self.oldest_height.store(keep_from_height, Ordering::SeqCst);\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// ---------- High-level helpers for specific Symphony domains ---------- //\n\nimpl StateDb {\n    /// Convenience wrapper around `get` dedicated to `AccountState` lookups.\n    pub fn get_account(&self, address: &Address) -> Result<Option<AccountState>, StateDbError> {\n        self.get::<AccountState>(address)\n    }\n\n    /// Store an entire `AccountState` at the next block height.\n    pub fn set_account(\n        &self,\n        address: &Address,\n        account: &AccountState,\n    ) -> Result<StateRoot, StateDbError> {\n        self.commit_block::<AccountState>(WriteSet::from([WriteOp::Put(\n            address.to_vec(),\n            account.clone(),\n        )]))\n    }\n\n    /// Retrieve arbitrary contract storage key for a given contract `address`.\n    pub fn get_contract_storage<V: DeserializeOwned>(\n        &self,\n        address: &Address,\n        storage_key: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<Option<V>, StateDbError> {\n        let mut composite = Vec::from(address.as_slice());\n        composite.extend_from_slice(storage_key);\n        self.get::<V>(&composite)\n    }\n\n    /// Put a value under contract storage.\n    pub fn set_contract_storage<V: Serialize>(\n        &self,\n        address: &Address,\n        storage_key: &[u8],\n        value: &V,\n    ) -> Result<StateRoot, StateDbError> {\n        let mut composite = Vec::from(address.as_slice());\n        composite.extend_from_slice(storage_key);\n        self.commit_block::<V>(WriteSet::from([WriteOp::Put(composite, value.clone())]))\n    }\n}\n\n// ----------------------- Tests ----------------------- //\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use rand::Rng;\n    use tempfile::TempDir;\n\n    fn random_address() -> Address {\n        rand::thread_rng().gen()\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn basic_read_write_account() {\n        let tmp = TempDir::new().expect(\"tmp dir\");\n        let db = StateDb::open(tmp.path()).unwrap();\n\n        let addr = random_address();\n        let mut acct = AccountState::default();\n        acct.balance = 42;\n\n        let root1 = db.set_account(&addr, &acct).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(db.get_account(&addr).unwrap(), Some(acct.clone()));\n\n        acct.balance = 1337;\n        let root2 = db.set_account(&addr, &acct).unwrap();\n        assert_eq!(db.get_account(&addr).unwrap(), Some(acct));\n\n        assert_ne!(root1, root2);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn pruning_works() {\n        let tmp = TempDir::new().unwrap();\n        let db = StateDb::open(tmp.path()).unwrap();\n        let addr = random_address();\n        let acct = AccountState::default();\n\n        // write 5 blocks\n        for _ in 0..5 {\n            db.set_account(&addr, &acct).unwrap();\n        }\n\n        // prune first 3\n        db.prune(3).unwrap();\n\n        // requesting block 2 should fail\n        assert!(matches!(\n            db.get_at::<AccountState>(2, &addr),\n            Err(StateDbError::Pruned { .. })\n        ));\n\n        // latest works\n        assert!(db.get_account(&addr).unwrap().is_some());\n    }\n}\n```",

This file purposefully contains no gRPC or HTTP\n//! plumbing;  it is meant to be embedded by the service\u2010layer binary and\n//! driven by the surrounding transport / storage adapters.\n//!\n//! Architectural notes\n//! -------------------\n//! \u2022 State is kept in-memory behind a `RwLock` and checkpointed by the\n//!   service into persistent storage (e.g. Postgres, RocksDB) \u2013 that part is\n//!   out-of-scope here.\n//! \u2022 Composer selection follows a simplified Proof-of-Inspiration algorithm:\n//!      1. Each staker submits a *VRF proof* for a given round\u2010seed.\n//!      2. The hash output is mapped to `[0, 1)`.  The staker wins if\n//!         output / stake_total < staker_weight.\n//!      3. Ties are broken deterministically by lowest hash.\n//! \u2022 A Strategy pattern exposes pluggable `VrfProvider`s so that collectives\n//!   can experiment with different curves (Ed25519, BLS, PQ, \u2026) without\n//!   recompilation of the other micro-services.\n\nuse std::{\n    collections::HashMap,\n    sync::Arc,\n    time::{Duration, SystemTime},\n};\n\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse rand::{rngs::OsRng, RngCore};\nuse sha2::{Digest, Sha256};\nuse tokio::{\n    sync::{broadcast, RwLock},\n    time,\n};\n\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Unique user/staker identifier (e.g. wallet address).\npub type StakerId = String;\n/// Result shorthand used throughout the stake logic.\npub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, StakingError>;\n\n/// Public event types that can be subscribed to by other micro-services\n/// through the event-bus (`broadcast::Sender`).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum StakingEvent {\n    StakeAdded {\n        staker: StakerId,\n        amount: u128,\n        new_total: u128,\n    },\n    StakeWithdrawn {\n        staker: StakerId,\n        amount: u128,\n        new_total: u128,\n    },\n    ComposerSelected {\n        round: u64,\n        staker: StakerId,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Domain errors emitted by staking logic.\n#[derive(Error, Debug)]\npub enum StakingError {\n    #[error(\"insufficient stake: requested {requested}, available {available}\")]\n    InsufficientStake { requested: u128, available: u128 },\n    #[error(\"staker `{0}` is not registered\")]\n    UnknownStaker(StakerId),\n    #[error(\"VRF verification failed: {0}\")]\n    VrfFailed(String),\n    #[error(\"no stakers registered\")]\n    EmptyPool,\n    #[error(\"attempted to withdraw zero tokens\")]\n    ZeroWithdrawal,\n}\n\n/// Represents an individual staking participant.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Staker {\n    pub id: StakerId,\n    pub stake: u128,\n    pub last_active: DateTime<Utc>,\n    pub vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>, // curve is provider specific\n}\n\nimpl Staker {\n    fn new(id: StakerId, initial: u128, vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            id,\n            stake: initial,\n            last_active: Utc::now(),\n            vrf_pubkey,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Abstraction for a Verifiable Random Function provider.\npub trait VrfProvider: Send + Sync + 'static {\n    /// Produces a VRF proof and output hash for `message` using the *private*\n    /// part of the provider implementation.\n    fn prove(&self, message: &[u8]) -> (Vec<u8> /*proof*/, Vec<u8> /*hash*/);\n\n    /// Verify a proof & hash produced by `prove`.\n    fn verify(\n        &self,\n        public_key: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        proof: &[u8],\n        hash: &[u8],\n    ) -> std::result::Result<(), String>;\n}\n\n/// Fallback VRF provider that is *not* secure; meant only for local-dev and\n/// CI where cryptography isn\u2019t the focus.  It deterministically hashes the\n/// message + static `private_key`.\npub struct Sha256Vrf {\n    private_key: Vec<u8>,\n}\n\nimpl Sha256Vrf {\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        let mut pk = vec![0u8; 32];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut pk);\n        Self { private_key: pk }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl VrfProvider for Sha256Vrf {\n    fn prove(&self, message: &[u8]) -> (Vec<u8>, Vec<u8>) {\n        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n        hasher.update(&self.private_key);\n        hasher.update(message);\n        let hash = hasher.finalize().to_vec();\n        // `proof` is meaningless here \u2011 we return the key for \u201cverification\u201d\n        (self.private_key.clone(), hash)\n    }\n\n    fn verify(\n        &self,\n        public_key: &[u8],\n        message: &[u8],\n        proof: &[u8],\n        hash: &[u8],\n    ) -> std::result::Result<(), String> {\n        if public_key != proof {\n            return Err(\"public key mismatch\".into());\n        }\n        let mut hasher = Sha256::new();\n        hasher.update(proof); // same as private_key in this dummy impl\n        hasher.update(message);\n        let expected = hasher.finalize();\n        if expected.as_slice() == hash {\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(\"hash mismatch\".into())\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Shared staking state guarded by `RwLock`.\n#[derive(Default)]\nstruct StakePoolInner {\n    stakers: HashMap<StakerId, Staker>,\n    total_stake: u128,\n    current_round: u64,\n}\n\n/// Public handle for performing staking operations + composer selection.\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct StakePool {\n    inner: Arc<RwLock<StakePoolInner>>,\n    vrf: Arc<dyn VrfProvider>,\n    event_tx: broadcast::Sender<StakingEvent>,\n}\n\nimpl StakePool {\n    /// Create a new [`StakePool`] with the provided `VrfProvider`.\n    pub fn new(vrf: Arc<dyn VrfProvider>) -> Self {\n        let (event_tx, _) = broadcast::channel(256);\n        Self {\n            inner: Arc::default(),\n            vrf,\n            event_tx,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Subscribe to [`StakingEvent`]s.\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> broadcast::Receiver<StakingEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n\n    /// Register a new staker or top-up their existing stake.\n    pub async fn add_stake(\n        &self,\n        staker_id: StakerId,\n        vrf_pubkey: Vec<u8>,\n        amount: u128,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n\n        let entry = inner.stakers.entry(staker_id.clone()).or_insert_with(|| {\n            Staker::new(staker_id.clone(), 0, vrf_pubkey.clone())\n        });\n\n        entry.stake = entry.stake.saturating_add(amount);\n        entry.last_active = Utc::now();\n        inner.total_stake = inner.total_stake.saturating_add(amount);\n\n        self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::StakeAdded {\n            staker: staker_id,\n            amount,\n            new_total: entry.stake,\n        }).ok();\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Withdraw stake.  Fails if the caller tries to withdraw more than they have.\n    pub async fn withdraw_stake(&self, staker_id: &str, amount: u128) -> Result<()> {\n        if amount == 0 {\n            return Err(StakingError::ZeroWithdrawal);\n        }\n\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n        let staker = inner\n            .stakers\n            .get_mut(staker_id)\n            .ok_or_else(|| StakingError::UnknownStaker(staker_id.into()))?;\n\n        if staker.stake < amount {\n            return Err(StakingError::InsufficientStake {\n                requested: amount,\n                available: staker.stake,\n            });\n        }\n\n        staker.stake -= amount;\n        staker.last_active = Utc::now();\n        inner.total_stake -= amount;\n\n        self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::StakeWithdrawn {\n            staker: staker_id.into(),\n            amount,\n            new_total: staker.stake,\n        }).ok();\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Internal helper to draw a random seed for the next composer round.\n    fn next_round_seed() -> [u8; 32] {\n        let mut seed = [0u8; 32];\n        OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut seed);\n        seed\n    }\n\n    /// Schedule automatic composer selection every `interval`.\n    pub async fn run_composer_election(self: Arc<Self>, interval: Duration) {\n        let mut ticker = time::interval(interval);\n\n        loop {\n            ticker.tick().await;\n            let seed = Self::next_round_seed();\n            match self.select_composer(seed).await {\n                Ok(Some(winner)) => {\n                    tracing::info!(round = self.current_round().await, %winner, \"composer selected\");\n                }\n                Ok(None) => {\n                    // pool is empty\n                }\n                Err(e) => tracing::error!(\"failed to select composer: {e}\"),\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Return current round number without locking write.\n    pub async fn current_round(&self) -> u64 {\n        self.inner.read().await.current_round\n    }\n\n    /// Execute a single composer election round with the provided seed.\n    /// Returns `Ok(Some(staker_id))` on success, `Ok(None)` if pool empty.\n    /// State changes (round increment) are committed atomically.\n    pub async fn select_composer(&self, seed: [u8; 32]) -> Result<Option<StakerId>> {\n        let mut inner = self.inner.write().await;\n\n        if inner.stakers.is_empty() {\n            return Ok(None);\n        }\n\n        let message = seed; // serialized seed acts as VRF message\n        let mut best_candidate: Option<(StakerId, Vec<u8>)> = None;\n\n        for staker in inner.stakers.values() {\n            // Build domain-separated message: seed || staker-id\n            let mut msg_vec = message.to_vec();\n            msg_vec.extend(staker.id.as_bytes());\n\n            // Each candidate derives a VRF output (hash) \u2013 prove/verify may\n            // happen off-chain in a real system; we shortcut here.\n            let (_proof, hash) = self.vrf.prove(&msg_vec);\n\n            // Map first 16 bytes \u2192 u128 for uniform comparison\n            let mut buf = [0u8; 16];\n            buf.copy_from_slice(&hash[..16]);\n            let rnd = u128::from_be_bytes(buf);\n\n            // Calculate target: (rnd / 2^128) < (stake / total)\n            // Reorder: rnd * total < stake * 2^128\n            let left = rnd.saturating_mul(inner.total_stake);\n            let right = staker.stake.saturating_mul(u128::MAX);\n\n            let eligible = left < right;\n            if eligible {\n                // Keep the lowest hash to break ties deterministically\n                match &mut best_candidate {\n                    None => best_candidate = Some((staker.id.clone(), hash)),\n                    Some((_best_id, best_hash)) => {\n                        if hash < *best_hash {\n                            *best_hash = hash;\n                            *_best_id = staker.id.clone();\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        inner.current_round += 1;\n\n        if let Some((winner, _)) = &best_candidate {\n            self.event_tx\n                .send(StakingEvent::ComposerSelected {\n                    round: inner.current_round,\n                    staker: winner.clone(),\n                })\n                .ok();\n        }\n\n        Ok(best_candidate.map(|(id, _)| id))\n    }\n\n    /// Utility used primarily by tests & admin dashboards.\n    pub async fn snapshot(&self) -> (u128, Vec<Staker>) {\n        let inner = self.inner.read().await;\n        (inner.total_stake, inner.stakers.values().cloned().collect())\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::collections::HashSet;\n\n    #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_stake_add_withdraw() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n        pool.add_stake(\"alice\".into(), vec![1, 2, 3], 1_000).await.unwrap();\n        pool.add_stake(\"bob\".into(), vec![4, 5, 6], 2_000).await.unwrap();\n        let (total, _) = pool.snapshot().await;\n        assert_eq!(total, 3_000);\n\n        pool.withdraw_stake(\"bob\", 500).await.unwrap();\n        let (total, stakers) = #[tokio::test]\n    async fn test_composer_selection() {\n        let pool = StakePool::new(Arc::new(Sha256Vrf::new()));\n        // Ensure deterministic test by using static VRF keys\n        pool.add_stake(\"alice\".into(), vec![1; 32], 1_000).await.unwrap();\n        pool.add_stake(\"bob\".into(), vec![2; 32], 10_000).await.unwrap();\n\n        let seed = [42u8; 32];\n        let winner shared by helpers contained in this crate.\n///\n/// NB: the enum is kept deliberately small; specialised subsystems should\n/// create their own error enums and simply `#[from]` this one where needed.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum CcsCommonError {\n    /// Malformed address or ID strings.\n    #[error(\"Malformed data: {0}\")]\n    Malformed(String),\n\n    /// Hex decoding failure.\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Hex(#[from] hex::FromHexError),\n\n    /// UUID parsing failure.\n    #[error(transparent)]\n    Uuid(#[from] uuid::Error),\n\n    /// Catch-all variant for misc. string Copy, Clone, Default, Hash, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Serialize, Deserialize,\n)]\npub struct Address([u8; 32]);\n\nimpl Address {\n    pub const LEN: usize = 32;\n\n    #[inline]\n    pub fn {\n        self.0\n    }\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Address {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(f, \"0x{}\", self.0.encode_hex::<String>())\n return Err(CcsCommonError::Malformed(format!(\n                \"address length mismatch (expected {} hex chars, got {})\",\n                Self::LEN * 2,\n                raw.len()\n            )));\n        }\n\n        let bytes = <[u8; Self::LEN]>::from_hex(raw)?;\n        Ok(Self(bytes))\n    }\n}\n\n/// A globally unique 64-bit identifier for NFTs and fungible token classes.\n///\n/// By convention:\n///   - upper 16 bits encode a micro-service namespace\n///   - lower 48 bits are an incrementing counter\n#[derive(\n    Copy, Clone, Debug, Default, Hash, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, }\n}\n\n/// 256-bit content hash (CIDv1 raw-binary multihash).\n///\n/// Serialised as [base58btc] to remain URL-safe and human-friendly.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Hash, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, )]\n    pub [u8; 32],\n);\n\nimpl ContentHash {\n    pub fn new(bytes: [u8; 32]) -> Self {\n        Self(bytes)\n    }\n\n    pub fn as_bytes(&self) -> &[u8; 32] {\n        &self.0\n    }\n}\n\nimpl }\n}\n\n/// Unique identifier grouping a set of on-chain operations that form a single\n/// artistic \u201cmovement\u201d.\n#[derive(\n    Copy, Clone, Debug, Hash, PartialEq, Eq, Ord, PartialOrd, \"custom-{}\", id),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Signature curve algorithms supported by the Strategy pattern.\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"snake_case\")]\npub enum CurveAlgo {\n    Ed25519,\n    Sr25519,\n    Secp256k1,\n    Bls12381,\n    PostQuantumDilithium,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for CurveAlgo {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        use CurveAlgo::*;\n        let name = match self {\n            Ed25519 => \"ed25519\",\n            Sr25519 => \"sr25519\",\n            Secp256k1 => \"secp256k1\",\n            Bls12381 => \"bls12381\",\n            PostQuantumDilithium => \"pq-dilithium\",\n        };\n        f.write_str(name)\n    }\n}\n\n// serialize_b58<S>(bytes: &[u8; 32], ser: S) -> Result<S::Ok, S::Error>\n    where\n        S: Serializer,\n    {\n        ser.serialize_str(&bs58::encode(bytes).into_string())\n    }\n\n    pub fn deserialize_b58<'de, D>(de: D) -> Result<[u8; 32], D::Error>\n    where\n        D: Deserializer<'de>,\n    {\n        let s = String::deserialize(de)?;\n        let vec = bs58::decode(&s).into_vec().map_err(D::Error::custom)?;\n        if vec.len() != 32 {\n            return Err(D::Error::custom(format!(\n                \"invalid length: expected 32 bytes, got {}\",\n                vec.len()\n            )));\n        }\n        let mut bytes = [0u8; 32];\n        bytes.copy_from_slice(&vec);\n        Ok(bytes)\n    }\n}\n```",

The F-NFT feature will allow high-value multi-layer NFTs to be \"sharded\" into multiple fungible tokens, enabling fractional ownership, increased liquidity, and broader accessibility to premium digital art assets.\n\nThe design follows the existing microservices architecture using gRPC for inter-service communication and NATS JetStream for event-driven messaging, as established in ADR-001 and ADR-002.\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. `MultiLayerNft` when it has been sharded.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalInfo {\n    /// Unique identifier for the fraction token series\n    pub fraction_token_id: Uuid,\n\n    /// Total number of fractions (shares) created\n    pub total_supply: u64,\n\n    /// Current circulating supply (may differ if some burned)\n    pub pub fractionalized_at: u64,\n\n    /// Address that initiated the fractionalization\n    pub fractionalizer: WalletAddress,\n\n    /// Whether the NFT can be reconstituted (all fractions returned to one owner)\n    pub reconstitutable: bool,\n\n    /// Buyout price in platform tokens (optional, for forced buyout mechanism)\n    pub buyout_price: Option<TokenAmount>,\n\n    /// Current state of the fractional NFT\n    pub state: FractionalState,\n}\n\n/// State machine for fractional NFT lifecycle\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum FractionalState {\n    /// Fractionalization is pending (in mempool)\n    Pending,\n    /// NFT is actively fractionalized\n    Active,\n    /// Buyout initiated, fractions can be redeemed\n    BuyoutInProgress { initiator: WalletAddress, deadline: u64 },\n    /// NFT has been reconstituted to a single owner\n    Reconstituted,\n    /// Fractionalized NFT has been dissolved (rare edge key = Self::FRACTION_PREFIX.to_vec();\n        key.extend_from_slice(token_id);\n        key.extend_from_slice(wallet.as_bytes());\n        key\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Component-Level Design\n\n### 3.1 Node Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/node_service/src/state_machine.rs`\n\n**New Transaction Types:**\n\n```rust\n/// Extended NodeEvent enum with F-NFT events\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub enum NodeEvent {\n    // Existing events...\n    Tick,\n    PeerConnected(PeerId),\n    BlockReceived(Block),\n    ElectedComposer,\n    Shutdown,\n\n    // NEW: Fractionalization events\n    FractionalizeNft {\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        owner: WalletAddress,\n        total_fractions: u64,\n        min_trade_unit: u64,\n        signature: Vec<u8>,\n    },\n    TransferFractions {\n        fraction_token_id: Uuid,\n        from: WalletAddress,\n        to: WalletAddress,\n        amount: u64,\n        signature: Vec<u8>,\n    },\n    InitiateBuyout {\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        initiator: WalletAddress,\n        offered_price: TokenAmount,\n    },\n    ReconstituteFractionalNft {\n        nft_id: Uuid,\n        owner: WalletAddress, // Must own 100% of fractions\n    },\n}\n```\n\n**State Transition Logic:**\n\nAdd to `StateActive::on_event`:\n\n```rust\n// In StateActive implementation\nasync fn on_event(&mut self, ctx: &mut NodeContext, event: NodeEvent) -> anyhow::Result<Transition> {\n    match event {\n        // ... existing handlers ...\n\n        NodeEvent::FractionalizeNft { nft_id, owner, total_fractions, min_trade_unit, signature } => {\n            // 1. Verify ownership\n            // 2. Verify NFT is not already fractionalized\n            // 3. Verify NFT layers are not frozen (or handle appropriately)\n            // 4. Create FractionalInfo\n            // 5. Mint fraction tokens to owner\n            // 6. Update state and publish event\n            handle_fractionalize(ctx, nft_id, owner, total_fractions, min_trade_unit, signature).await?;\n            Ok(Transition::Stay)\n        }\n\n        NodeEvent::TransferFractions { fraction_token_id, from, to, amount, signature } => {\n            // 1. Verify signature\n            // 2. Check balance\n            // 3. Execute transfer\n            // 4. Emit event\n            handle_fraction_transfer(ctx, fraction_token_id, from, to, amount, signature).await?;\n            Ok(Transition::Stay)\n        }\n        // ... more handlers\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/node_service/src/mempool.rs`\n\nAdd validation for fractionalization transactions:\n\n```rust\nimpl Mempool {\n    /// Validate a fractionalization transaction before adding to mempool\n    pub fn validate_fractionalize_tx(\n        &self,\n        nft_id: &Uuid,\n        owner: &WalletAddress,\n        total_fractions: u64,\n    ) -> Result<(), MempoolError> {\n        // 1. Minimum fractions check (e.g., >= 2)\n        if total_fractions < 2 {\n            return Err(MempoolError::InvalidFractionCount);\n        }\n\n        // 2. Maximum fractions check (prevent gas attacks)\n        if total_fractions > 1_000_000_000 {\n            return Err(MempoolError::ExcessiveFractionCount);\n        }\n\n        // 3. Check NFT exists and is owned by sender\n        // 4. Check NFT is not already fractionalized\n        // 5. Check no pending fractionalize tx for this NFT\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Minting Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs`\n\n**New Methods:**\n\n```rust\nimpl<S, C, E> NftFactory<S, C, E>\nwhere\n    S: CryptoSigner + 'static,\n    C: BlockchainClient + 'static,\n    E: EventPublisher + 'static,\n{\n    /// Fractionalize an existing NFT into fungible fraction tokens\n    #[instrument(skip_all, level = \"info\", fields(nft_id = %req.nft_id))]\n    pub async fn fractionalize_nft(&self, req: FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<FractionalizeResponse, FactoryError> {\n        // 1. Validate the request\n        self.validate_fractionalize_request(&req)?;\n\n        // 2. Build fractionalization payload\n        let fraction_token_id = Uuid::new_v4();\n        let payload = self.build_fractionalize_payload(&req, &fraction_token_id).await?;\n\n        // 3. Sign the payload\n        let signature = self.signer.sign(&payload).await?;\n\n        // 4. Submit to chain\n        let tx_hash = self.chain.submit_fractionalize(FractionalizePayload {\n            nft_id: req.nft_id.clone(),\n            fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n            total_fractions: req.total_fractions,\n            min_trade_unit: req.min_trade_unit,\n            reconstitutable: req.reconstitutable,\n            buyout_price: req.buyout_price,\n            signature,\n        }).await?;\n\n        // 5. Publish success event\n        self.bus.publish(\n            &self.config.event_topic_fractionalized,\n            &FractionalizedEvent {\n                nft_id: req.nft_id.clone(),\n                fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n                total_fractions: req.total_fractions,\n                owner: req.owner_wallet.clone(),\n                timestamp_ms: now_millis(),\n            },\n        ).await?;\n\n        Ok(FractionalizeResponse {\n            fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n            tx_hash,\n            success: true,\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn validate_fractionalize_request(&self, req: &FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<(), FactoryError> {\n        if req.total_fractions < 2 {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"must create at least 2 fractions\".into()));\n        }\n        if req.total_fractions > self.config.max_fractions {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(format!(\n                \"cannot exceed {} fractions\",\n                self.config.max_fractions\n            )));\n        }\n        if req.min_trade_unit == 0 || req.min_trade_unit > req.total_fractions {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid min_trade_unit\".into()));\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/minting_service/src/rpc_server.rs`\n\n**New gRPC Endpoint:**\n\n```rust\n/// gRPC service implementation for fractionalization\n#[tonic::async_trait]\nimpl FractionalService for MintingRpcServer {\n    async fn fractionalize(\n        &self,\n        request: Request<FractionalizeRequest>,\n    ) -> Result<Response<FractionalizeResponse>, Status> {\n        let req = request.into_inner();\n\n        // Validate signature\n        self.verify_signature(&req.owner_wallet, &req.signature).await\n            .map_err(|e| Status::unauthenticated(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        // Execute fractionalization\n        let response = self.factory\n            .fractionalize_nft(req)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| Status::internal(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        Ok(Response::new(response))\n    }\n\n    async fn reconstitute(\n        &self,\n        request: Request<ReconstituteRequest>,\n    ) -> Result<Response<ReconstituteResponse>, Status> {\n        // Handle NFT reconstitution when one owner has all fractions\n        // ...\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Wallet Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/wallet_service/src/key_manager.rs`\n\n**Extended ListingRepository> ListingManager<R> {\n    /// Create a listing for fraction tokens\n    pub async fn create_fraction_listing(\n        &self,\n        owner: AccountId,\n        fraction_token_id: String,\n        parent_nft_id: String,\n        amount: u64,\n        price_per_unit: Decimal,\n    ) -> Result<ListingId, ListingError> {\n        // Validate owner has sufficient fraction balance\n        // Create listing with ListingType::FractionTokens\n        // Escrow the fractions (transfer to marketplace contract)\n        // Emit ListingCreated event with fraction metadata\n\n        let listing = Listing {\n            id: ListingId::new(),\n            owner,\n            listing_type: ListingType::FractionTokens {\n                fraction_token_id,\n                parent_nft_id,\n                amount,\n                price_per_unit,\n            },\n            price: price_per_unit * Decimal::from(amount),\n            status: ListingStatus::Active,\n            created_at: Utc::now(),\n            updated_at: Utc::now(),\n        };\n\n        timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.insert(listing.clone()))\n            .await\n            .map_err(|_| pub async fn purchase_fractions(\n        &self,\n        listing_id: ListingId,\n        buyer: AccountId,\n        amount: u64,  // Can be partial purchase\n    ) -> Result<(), ListingError> {\n        let listing = self.repo.get(listing_id).await?;\n\n        // Validate listing is for fractions\n        let (fraction_token_id, available, price_per_unit) = match &listing.listing_type {\n            ListingType::FractionTokens { fraction_token_id, amount, price_per_unit, .. } => {\n                (fraction_token_id.clone(), *amount, *price_per_unit)\n            }\n            _ => return Err(ListingError::NotActive),\n        };\n\n        if amount > available {\n            return Err(ListingError::InsufficientQuantity);\n        }\n\n        // Calculate payment\n        let payment = price_per_unit * Decimal::from(amount);\n\n        // Execute atomic transfer: tokens -> buyer, payment -> seller\n        // Update or close listing based on remaining amount\n        // Emit event\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs`\n\n**Extended Auction Support:**\n\n```rust\n/// Extended CreateAuction to support File: `services/governance_service/src/proposal_engine.rs`\n\n**Weighted Voting with Fractions:**\n\n```rust\nimpl<S, E, V> ProposalEngine<S, E, V>\nwhere\n    S: ProposalStore,\n    E: EventPublisher,\n    V: SignatureVerifier,\n{\n    /// Cast a vote with weight calculated from NFT + fraction holdings\n    pub async fn cast_weighted_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        // Verify signature\n        // ...\n\n        // Calculate voting weight from:\n        // 1. Whole NFT holdings\n        // 2. Fractional NFT holdings (proportional to ownership percentage)\n        let voting_weight = self.calculate_voting_power(voter).await?;\n\n        // Store vote with weight\n        self.store\n            .save_weighted_vote(proposal_id, voter, choice, voting_weight)\n            .await?;\n\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::WeightedVoteCast {\n                proposal_id,\n                voter: voter.to_owned(),\n                choice,\n                weight: voting_weight,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate voting power including fractional ownership\n    async fn calculate_voting_power(&self, voter: &str) -> Result<u64, ProposalError> {\n        // Get whole NFT count\n        let whole_nft_power = self.get_whole_nft_count(voter).await? * 100;\n\n        // Get fractional holdings and sum weighted by ownership %\n        let fraction_holdings = self.get_fraction_holdings(voter).await?;\n        let fraction_power: u64 = fraction_holdings\n            .iter()\n            .map(|h| {\n                let ownership_pct = (h.balance as f64 / h.total_supply as f64) * 100.0;\n                ownership_pct as u64\n            })\n            .sum();\n\n        Ok(whole_nft_power + fraction_power)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Modified Outcome Calculation:**\n\n```rust\n/// Computes outcome using weighted votes\nfn compute_weighted_outcome(proposal: &Proposal, params: &GovernanceParameters) -> ProposalOutcome {\n    let total_weight: u64 = proposal.weighted_votes.values().map(|(_, w)| w).sum();\n\n    if total_weight == 0 {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_weight: u64 = proposal\n        .weighted_votes\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|(_, (choice, _))| *choice == VoteChoice::Yes)\n        .map(|(_, (_, weight))| weight)\n        .sum();\n\n    let quorum_met = total_weight >= params.required_quorum_weight;\n\n    if !quorum_met {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_pct = (yes_weight * 100) / total_weight;\n    if yes_pct >= params.pass_threshold_pct as u64 {\n        ProposalOutcome::Accepted\n    } else {\n        ProposalOutcome::Rejected\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.6 Staking Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs`\n\n**Fraction-Aware Staking:**\n\n```rust\nimpl StakePool {\n    /// Calculate staking rewards distribution including fraction holders\n    pub async fn distribute_rewards_to_fraction_holders(\n        &self,\n        nft_id: &Uuid,\n        total_reward: u128,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<(StakerId, u128)>, StakingError> {\n        // Get all fraction holders for this NFT\n        let holders = self.get_fraction_holders(nft_id).await?;\n\n        // Calculate each holder's share proportionally\n        let distributions: Vec<(StakerId, u128)> = holders\n            .iter()\n            .map(|(staker_id, balance, total_supply)| {\n                let share = (total_reward * *balance as u128) / *total_supply as u128;\n                (staker_id.clone(), share)\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Emit distribution events\n        for (staker, amount) in &distributions {\n            self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::FractionRewardDistributed {\n                nft_id: nft_id.to_string(),\n                staker: staker.clone(),\n                amount: *amount,\n            }).ok();\n        }\n\n        Ok(distributions)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.7 API Gateway Changes\n\n#### File: `services/api_gateway/src/rest_api.rs`\n\n**New REST Endpoints:**\n\n```rust\npub fn payload))]\nasync fn fractionalize_nft(\n    State(state): State<AppState>,\n    Path(nft_id): Path<String>,\n    headers: HeaderMap,\n    Json(payload): Json<FractionalizeRequestBody>,\n) -> Result<impl IntoResponse, ApiError> {\n    // Validate request\n    if payload.total_fractions < 2 {\n        return Err(ApiError::BadRequest(\"must create at least 2 fractions\".into()));\n    }\n\n    // Forward to minting service via gRPC\n    let grpc_req = tonic::Request::new(proto::fractional::FractionalizeRequest {\n        nft_id,\n        owner_wallet: payload.owner_wallet,\n        total_fractions: payload.total_fractions,\n        min_trade_unit: payload.min_trade_unit.unwrap_or(1),\n        reconstitutable: payload.reconstitutable.unwrap_or(true),\n        buyout_price: payload.buyout_price,\n        signature: payload.signature,\n    });\n\n    let response = state.minting.clone()\n        .fractionalize(grpc_req)\n        .await?\n        .into_inner();\n\n    Ok((\n        StatusCode::CREATED,\n        Json(FractionalizeResponseBody {\n            fraction_token_id: response.fraction_token_id,\n            tx_hash: response.tx_hash,\n            success: response.success,\n        }),\n    ))\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"camelCase\")]\nstruct FractionalizeRequestBody {\n    pub owner_wallet: String,\n    pub total_fractions: u64,\n    pub min_trade_unit: Option<u64>,\n    pub reconstitutable: Option<bool>,\n    pub buyout_price: Option<u64>,\n    pub signature: Vec<u8>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"camelCase\")]\nstruct FractionalizeResponseBody {\n    pub fraction_token_id: String,\n    pub tx_hash: String,\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/api_gateway/src/grpc_client.rs`\n\n**Extended gRPC Client:**\n\n```rust\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct AppState {\n    pub minting: MintingServiceClient<Channel>,\n    pub composition: })\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Core User Flows\n\n### 4.1 Flow: Owner Fractionalizing an Existing NFT\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502   Client    \u2502    \u2502  API Gateway  \u2502    \u2502 Minting Service \u2502    \u2502 Node Service \u2502    \u2502  State DB    \u2502\n\u2502   (DApp)    \u2502    \u2502  (REST API)   \u2502    \u2502    (gRPC)       \u2502    \u2502 (Consensus)  \u2502    \u2502  (sled)      \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502 1. POST /nfts/{id}/fractionalize        \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502   { totalFractions: 100, ... }          \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502 2. Validate request  \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502 3. gRPC: Fractionalize()                   \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 4. Validate NFT ownership              \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 5. Build fractionalize tx              \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 6. Sign with service key               \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 7. Submit tx: FractionalizeNft         \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502 8.
