Publish event\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502   (NATS JetStream)\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 14. Return tx_hash\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 15. Return response \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 16. 201 Created      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502   { fractionTokenId, txHash }           \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n```\n\n**Detailed Steps:**\n\n1. **Client Request**: User submits fractionalization request via DApp with:\n   - `nft_id`: The NFT to fractionalize\n   - `totalFractions`: Number of fractions to create (e.g., 100)\n   - `minTradeUnit`: Minimum tradeable unit (e.g., 1)\n   - `reconstitutable`: Whether NFT can be reconstituted\n   - `buyoutPrice`: Optional forced buyout price\n   - `signature`: Owner's signature authorizing the action\n\n2. **API Gateway Validation**: Validates request format, rate limits, authentication\n\n3. **gRPC Call**: Forwards to Minting Service's `Fractionalize` RPC\n\n4. **Ownership Verification**: Minting Service queries state to verify caller owns the NFT\n\n5. **Transaction Building**: Creates `FractionalizeNft` transaction payload\n\n6. **Signing**: Service signs the transaction with its operator key\n\n7. **Chain Submission**: Submits transaction to Node Service\n\n8. **Mempool Validation**: Node validates:\n   - NFT exists and is not already fractionalized\n   - Owner signature is valid\n   - Fraction count is within limits\n\n9. **Block Inclusion**: Transaction included in next block via Proof-of-Inspiration\n\n10. **State Transition**: `state_machine.rs` processes `FractionalizeNft` event\n\n11. **FractionalInfo Creation**: Creates and stores `FractionalInfo` struct attached to NFT\n\n12. **Fraction Minting**: Mints all fraction tokens to original owner's wallet\n\n13. **Event Publishing**: Publishes `nft.fractionalized` event to NATS JetStream\n\n14. **Response**: Returns transaction hash to Minting Service\n\n15. **gRPC Response**: Returns `FractionalizeResponse` to API Gateway\n\n16. **Client Response**: Returns success with `fraction_token_id` and `tx_hash`\n\n### 4.2 Flow: User Purchasing a Fraction on the Marketplace\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 Validate buyer has sufficient funds  \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502 9. Calculate payment amount             \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502 10. Create atomic transfer tx           \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502 11. Validate signatures\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502 12. Execute in block:\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502   a. Transfer payment seller -> escrow\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502   b. Transfer fractions escrow -> buyer\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502   c. Update listing status\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502 13. Update state \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502 14. Publish events:  \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502   - FractionTransferred                 \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502   - ListingPurchased \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 15. Return result \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 16. 200 OK           \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502   { txHash, fractionsAcquired: 10 }      \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n```\n\n**Detailed Steps:**\n\n1. **Browse Listings**: Buyer queries available fraction listings\n\n2. **gRPC Query**: API Gateway calls Marketplace Service's `ListFractionListings`\n\n3. **Database Query**: Marketplace queries listings repository\n\n4. **Return Listings**: Buyer sees available fractions with prices\n\n5. **Purchase Request**: Buyer submits purchase for 10 fractions from a listing\n\n6. **gRPC Purchase**: API Gateway calls `PurchaseFractions` RPC\n\n7. **Listing Validation**: Verify listing exists, is active, has sufficient quantity\n\n8. **Funds Validation**: Check buyer's wallet balance covers payment + gas\n\n9. **Payment Calculation**: `price_per_unit * amount = total_payment`\n\n10. **Atomic Transaction**: Create transaction with:\n    - Transfer payment from buyer to seller\n    - Transfer fractions from escrow to buyer\n    - Update or close listing\n\n11. **Transaction Validation**: Node validates all signatures and balances\n\n12. **Block Execution**: Execute atomic transfer in single block\n\n13. **State Update**: Update fraction ownership in state DB\n\n14. **Event Publishing**: Publish to NATS JetStream:\n    - `marketplace.fractions.purchased`\n    - `nft.fractions.transferred`\n\n15. **Result Return**: Return transaction result to Marketplace Service\n\n16. **Client Response**: Return success with transaction hash and acquired amount\n\n---\n\n## 5. (config/default.toml)\n\n```toml\n# Add new section for F-NFT configuration:\n\n#######################################################################\n# Fractional NFT Settings\n#######################################################################\n[fractional_nft]\n# Enable/disable fractional NFT feature\nenabled = true\n\n# Minimum number of fractions when fractionalizing\nmin_fractions = 2\n\n# Maximum number of fractions allowed per NFT\nmax_fractions = 1_000_000_000\n\n# Default minimum tradeable unit\ndefault_min_trade_unit = 1\n\n# Fee charged for fractionalization (in CANV)\nfractionalization_fee = \"1.0\"\n\n# Buyout mechanism settings\n[fractional_nft.buyout]\n# Allow forced buyout if one holder acquires threshold\nenabled = true\n# Minimum ownership percentage to initiate buyout\ninitiation_threshold = 90.0\n# Grace period for other holders to counter-offer (in seconds)\ngrace_period_secs = 604800  # 7 days\n# Premium above market price required for buyout\nminimum_premium_pct = 10.0\n\n# Reconstitution settings\n[fractional_nft.reconstitution]\n# Allow NFT reconstitution when 100% owned\nenabled = true\n# Fee for reconstitution (in CANV)\nreconstitution_fee = \"0.5\"\n\n# Governance integration\n[fractional_nft.governance]\n# How fractional holdings affect voting power\nvoting_weight_model = \"proportional\"  # or \"sqrt\", \"linear_capped\"\n# Cap on voting power from any single fractional position (0 = no cap)\nmax_voting_power_pct = 0\n\n# Marketplace integration\n[fractional_nft.marketplace]\n# Minimum listing price per fraction (in CANV)\nmin_listing_price = \"0.001\"\n# Platform fee on fraction sales (basis points)\nplatform_fee_bps = 250  # 2.5%\n# Royalty distribution to original creator (basis points)\ncreator_royalty_bps = 500  # 5%\n```\n\n### 5.3 Event Bus Configuration (NATS JetStream)\n\n```toml\n# Add to [event_bus] section:\n[event_bus]\n# Existing configuration...\nnats_url = \"nats://127.0.0.1:4222\"\nstream_name = \"CANVAS_EVENTS\"\n\n# Add new subjects for F-NFT events\nsubjects = {\n  nft_minted = \"nft.minted\",\n  vote_cast = \"gov.vote\",\n  payout = fraction_auction_bid = \"marketplace.fraction.auction.bid\",\n  fraction_auction_settled = \"marketplace.fraction.auction.settled\",\n  buyout_initiated = \"nft.buyout.initiated\",\n  buyout_completed = \"nft.buyout.completed\",\n  nft_reconstituted = \"nft.reconstituted\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Security Considerations\n\n### 6.1 Ownership Verification\n- All fractionalization requests must include a valid signature from the NFT owner\n- The `node_service` state machine must verify ownership before processing `FractionalizeNft` transactions\n- Double-spend protection via mempool validation (prevent racing fractionalization attempts)\n\n### 6.2 Atomic Transactions\n- All fraction transfers must be atomic (either complete fully or revert)\n- Marketplace purchases must atomically transfer both payment and fractions\n- Use database transactions in `ccs_db` to ensure consistency\n\n### 6.3 Buyout Protection\n- Implement time-locked buyout process with grace period for counter-offers\n- Require premium above market price for forced buyouts\n- Allow governance vote to block hostile buyout attempts\n\n### 6.4 Reconstitution Safeguards\n- Only allow reconstitution when holder owns exactly 100% of fractions\n- Prevent reconstitution during active auctions or pending transactions\n- Emit events for all reconstitution attempts for audit trail\n\n### 6.5 Rate Limiting\n- Apply rate limits to fractionalization requests (prevent DoS)\n- Limit number of active listings per wallet\n- Throttle fraction transfer frequency\n\n---\n\n## 7. Migration Strategy\n\n### 7.1 Database Migrations\n1. Add new columns/tables for fractional ownership tracking\n2. Deploy state_db schema changes during maintenance window\n3. Run migration scripts to index existing NFTs (mark as non-fractionalized)\n\n### 7.2 Service Deployment Order\n1. Deploy `ccs_common`, `ccs_proto`, `ccs_db` crate updates\n2. Deploy `node_service` with new transaction types (backwards compatible)\n3. Deploy `minting_service` with fractionalization endpoint\n4. Deploy `wallet_service` with fraction display support\n5. Deploy `marketplace_service` with fraction listing support\n6. Deploy `governance_service` with weighted voting\n7. Deploy `api_gateway` with new REST endpoints\n8. Enable feature flag in configuration\n\n### 7.3 Feature Flag Rollout\n- Use `[fractional_nft].enabled = false` initially\n- Enable for testnet validation\n- Gradual rollout to mainnet (canary deployment)\n- Full enablement after stability verification\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Impacted Files Summary\n\n### Critical Changes\n| File | Change Type | Priority   "content": "# Architectural Blueprint for Fractional NFT (F-NFT) Integration\n\n**CanvasChain Symphony - Technical Design Document**\n**Version**: 1.0.0\n**Date**: 2026-02-02\n**Author**: Lead Architect\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document provides a comprehensive architectural plan for integrating Fractional NFTs (F-NFTs) into the CanvasChain Symphony platform. The F-NFT feature will allow high-value multi-layer NFTs to be \"sharded\" into multiple fungible tokens, enabling fractional ownership, increased liquidity, and broader accessibility to premium digital art assets.\n\nThe design follows the existing microservices architecture using gRPC for inter-service communication and NATS JetStream for event-driven messaging, as established in ADR-001 and ADR-002.\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Impact Analysis](#1-impact-analysis)\n2. [Data Model Changes](#2-data-model-changes)\n3. [Component-Level Design](#3-component-level-design)\n4. [Core User Flows](#4-core-user-flows)\n5. [API & Configuration Changes](#5-api--configuration-changes)\n6. [Security Considerations](#6-security-considerations)\n7. [Migration Strategy](#7-migration-strategy)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Impact Analysis\n\n### 1.1 Impacted Services\n\n| Service | Impact Level | Description |\n|---------|--------------|-------------|\n| `node_service` | **Critical** | New transaction types for fractionalization and fraction transfers |\n| `minting_service` | **High** | New fractionalization endpoint, fraction token creation logic |\n| `wallet_service` | **High** | Display and manage fractional ownership positions |\n| `marketplace_service` | **High** | List, bid, and trade fraction tokens |\n| `governance_service` | **Medium** | Weighted voting based on fractional ownership |\n| `staking_service` | **Medium** | Staking rewards distribution for fraction holders |\n| `api_gateway` | **High** | New REST endpoints for F-NFT operations |\n| `royalty_service` | **Medium** | Royalty distribution to fraction holders |\n\n### 1.2 Impacted Shared Crates\n\n| Crate | Impact Level | Changes Required |\n|-------|--------------|------------------|\n| `ccs_common` | **Critical** | New `FractionalInfo` struct, `FractionalNft` type, modified `MultiLayerNft` |\n| `ccs_proto` | **High** | New protobuf messages for F-NFT operations |\n| `ccs_db` | **High** | New state storage for fractional ownership records |\n| `ccs_consensus` | **Medium** | Validation rules for fractionalization transactions |\n| `ccs_crypto` | **Low** | No changes (existing signature schemes sufficient) |\n\n### 1.3 Critical Files Impacted\n\n#### Core Domain (ccs_common)\n- `crates/ccs_common/src/nft.rs` - Auction fractional tokens\n\n#### Wallet Service\n- `services/wallet_service/src/key_manager.rs` - Manage fraction token balances\n- `services/wallet_service/src/rpc_server.rs` - Query fractional holdings\n\n#### Governance Service\n- `services/governance_service/src/proposal_engine.rs` - Data Model Changes\n\n### 2.1 Core Data Structures (ccs_common/src/nft.rs)\n\n#### New Struct: `FractionalInfo`\n\n```rust\n/// Metadata for a fractionalized NFT.\n/// This struct is attached to a `MultiLayerNft` when it has been sharded.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct FractionalInfo {\n    /// Unique identifier for the fraction token series\n    pub fraction_token_id: Uuid,\n\n    /// Total number of fractions (shares) created\n    pub total_supply: u64,\n\n    /// Current circulating supply (may differ if some burned)\n    pub circulating_supply: u64,\n\n    /// Minimum fraction units that can be traded (e.g., 1 = indivisible fractions)\n    pub min_trade_unit: u64,\n\n    /// Timestamp when fractionalization occurred\n    pub fractionalized_at: u64,\n\n    /// Address that initiated the fractionalization\n    pub fractionalizer: WalletAddress,\n\n    /// Whether the NFT can be reconstituted (all fractions returned to one owner)\n    pub reconstitutable: bool,\n\n    /// Buyout price in platform tokens (optional, for forced buyout mechanism)\n    pub buyout_price: Option<TokenAmount>,\n\n    /// Current state of the fractional NFT\n    pub state: FractionalState,\n}\n\n/// State machine for fractional NFT lifecycle\n#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum FractionalState {\n    /// Fractionalization is pending (in mempool)\n    Pending,\n    /// NFT is actively fractionalized\n    Active,\n    /// Buyout initiated, fractions can be redeemed\n    BuyoutInProgress { initiator: WalletAddress, deadline: u64 },\n    /// NFT has been reconstituted to a single owner\n    Reconstituted,\n    /// Fractionalized NFT has been dissolved (rare edge case)\n    Dissolved,\n}\n```\n\n#### Modified Struct: `MultiLayerNft`\n\n```rust\n/// The main multi-layer NFT object with optional fractionalization.\n#[derive(Clone, Debug, Serialize, Verify ownership\n            // 2. Verify NFT is not already fractionalized\n            // 3. Verify NFT layers are not frozen (or handle appropriately)\n            // 4. Create FractionalInfo\n            // 5. Mint fraction tokens to owner\n            // 6. Update state and publish event\n            handle_fractionalize(ctx, nft_id, owner, total_fractions, min_trade_unit, signature).await?;\n            Ok(Transition::Stay)\n        }\n\n        NodeEvent::TransferFractions { fraction_token_id, from, to, amount, signature } => {\n            // 1. Verify signature\n            // 2. Check balance\n            // 3. Execute transfer\n            // 4. Emit event\n            handle_fraction_transfer(ctx, fraction_token_id, from, to, amount, signature).await?;\n            Ok(Transition::Stay)\n        }\n        // ... more handlers\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/node_service/src/mempool.rs`\n\nAdd validation for fractionalization transactions:\n\n```rust\nimpl Mempool {\n    /// Validate a fractionalization transaction before adding to mempool\n    pub fn validate_fractionalize_tx(\n        &self,\n        nft_id: &Uuid,\n        owner: &WalletAddress,\n        total_fractions: u64,\n    ) -> Result<(), MempoolError> {\n        // 1. Minimum fractions check (e.g., >= 2)\n        if total_fractions < 2 {\n            return Err(MempoolError::InvalidFractionCount);\n        }\n\n        // 2. Maximum fractions check (prevent gas attacks)\n        if total_fractions > 1_000_000_000 {\n            return Err(MempoolError::ExcessiveFractionCount);\n        }\n\n        // 3. Check NFT exists and is owned by sender\n        // 4. Check NFT is not already fractionalized\n        // 5. Check no pending fractionalize tx for this NFT\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Minting Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/minting_service/src/logic/nft_factory.rs`\n\n**New Methods:**\n\n```rust\nimpl<S, C, E> NftFactory<S, C, E>\nwhere\n    S: CryptoSigner + 'static,\n    C: BlockchainClient + 'static,\n    E: EventPublisher + 'static,\n{\n    /// Fractionalize an existing NFT into fungible fraction tokens\n    #[instrument(skip_all, level = \"info\", fields(nft_id = %req.nft_id))]\n    pub async fn fractionalize_nft(&self, req: FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<FractionalizeResponse, FactoryError> {\n        // 1. Validate the request\n        self.validate_fractionalize_request(&req)?;\n\n        // 2. Build fractionalization payload\n        let fraction_token_id = Uuid::new_v4();\n        let payload = self.build_fractionalize_payload(&req, &fraction_token_id).await?;\n\n        // 3. Sign the payload\n        let signature = self.signer.sign(&payload).await?;\n\n        // 4. Submit to chain\n        let tx_hash = self.chain.submit_fractionalize(FractionalizePayload {\n            nft_id: req.nft_id.clone(),\n            fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n            total_fractions: req.total_fractions,\n            min_trade_unit: req.min_trade_unit,\n            reconstitutable: req.reconstitutable,\n            buyout_price: req.buyout_price,\n            signature,\n        }).await?;\n\n        // 5. Publish success event\n        self.bus.publish(\n            &self.config.event_topic_fractionalized,\n            &FractionalizedEvent {\n                nft_id: req.nft_id.clone(),\n                fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n                total_fractions: req.total_fractions,\n                owner: req.owner_wallet.clone(),\n                timestamp_ms: now_millis(),\n            },\n        ).await?;\n\n        Ok(FractionalizeResponse {\n            fraction_token_id: fraction_token_id.to_string(),\n            tx_hash,\n            success: true,\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn validate_fractionalize_request(&self, req: &FractionalizeRequest) -> Result<(), FactoryError> {\n        if req.total_fractions < 2 {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"must create at least 2 fractions\".into()));\n        }\n        if req.total_fractions > self.config.max_fractions {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(format!(\n                \"cannot exceed {} fractions\",\n                self.config.max_fractions\n            )));\n        }\n        if req.min_trade_unit == 0 || req.min_trade_unit > req.total_fractions {\n            return Err(FactoryError::Validation(\"invalid min_trade_unit\".into()));\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/minting_service/src/rpc_server.rs`\n\n**New gRPC Endpoint:**\n\n```rust\n/// gRPC service implementation for fractionalization\n#[tonic::async_trait]\nimpl FractionalService for MintingRpcServer {\n    async fn fractionalize(\n        &self,\n        request: Request<FractionalizeRequest>,\n    ) -> Result<Response<FractionalizeResponse>, Status> {\n        let req = request.into_inner();\n\n        // Validate signature\n        self.verify_signature(&req.owner_wallet, &req.signature).await\n            .map_err(|e| Status::unauthenticated(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        // Execute fractionalization\n        let response = self.factory\n            .fractionalize_nft(req)\n            .await\n            .map_err(|e| Status::internal(e.to_string()))?;\n\n        Ok(Response::new(response))\n    }\n\n    async fn reconstitute(\n        &self,\n        request: Request<ReconstituteRequest>,\n    ) -> Result<Response<ReconstituteResponse>, Status> {\n        // Handle NFT reconstitution when one owner has all fractions\n        // ...\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Wallet Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/wallet_service/src/key_manager.rs`\n\n**Extended ListingRepository> ListingManager<R> {\n    /// Create a listing for fraction tokens\n    pub async fn create_fraction_listing(\n        &self,\n        owner: AccountId,\n        fraction_token_id: String,\n        parent_nft_id: String,\n        amount: u64,\n        price_per_unit: Decimal,\n    ) -> Result<ListingId, ListingError> {\n        // Validate owner has sufficient fraction balance\n        // Create listing with ListingType::FractionTokens\n        // Escrow the fractions (transfer to marketplace contract)\n        // Emit ListingCreated event with fraction metadata\n\n        let listing = Listing {\n            id: ListingId::new(),\n            owner,\n            listing_type: ListingType::FractionTokens {\n                fraction_token_id,\n                parent_nft_id,\n                amount,\n                price_per_unit,\n            },\n            price: price_per_unit * Decimal::from(amount),\n            status: ListingStatus::Active,\n            created_at: Utc::now(),\n            updated_at: Utc::now(),\n        };\n\n        timeout(DB_OP_TIMEOUT, self.repo.insert(listing.clone()))\n            .await\n            .map_err(|_| ListingError::Timeout)??;\n\n        self.dispatch_event(MarketplaceEvent::FractionListingCreated(listing))?;\n\n        Ok(listing.id)\n    }\n\n    /// Purchase fraction tokens from a listing\n    pub async fn purchase_fractions(\n        &self,\n        listing_id: ListingId,\n        buyer: AccountId,\n        amount: u64,  // Can be partial purchase\n    ) -> Result<(), ListingError> {\n        let listing = self.repo.get(listing_id).await?;\n\n        // Validate listing is for fractions\n        let (fraction_token_id, available, price_per_unit) = match &listing.listing_type {\n            ListingType::FractionTokens { fraction_token_id, amount, price_per_unit, .. } => {\n                (fraction_token_id.clone(), *amount, *price_per_unit)\n            }\n            _ => return Err(ListingError::NotActive),\n        };\n\n        if amount > available {\n            return Err(ListingError::InsufficientQuantity);\n        }\n\n        // Calculate payment\n        let payment = price_per_unit * Decimal::from(amount);\n\n        // Execute atomic transfer: tokens -> buyer, payment -> seller\n        // Update or close listing based on remaining amount\n        // Emit event\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### File: `services/marketplace_service/src/auction_engine.rs`\n\n**Extended Auction Support:**\n\n```rust\n/// Extended CreateAuction to support fraction auctions\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub struct CreateAuction {\n    pub auction_type: AuctionAssetType,  // NEW\n    pub seller_id: UserId,\n    pub reserve_price: u128,\n    pub duration: Duration,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum AuctionAssetType {\n    WholeNft { nft_id: NftId },\n    FractionBundle {\n        fraction_token_id: String,\n        amount: u64,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl<S: AuctionStore> AuctionEngine<S> {\n    /// Create an auction for fraction tokens\n    pub async fn create_fraction_auction(\n        &self,\n        params: CreateFractionAuction,\n    ) -> Result<AuctionId, EngineError> {\n        // Similar to whole NFT auction but with fraction-specific validation\n        // Escrow the fractions\n        // Set up auction with per-unit or bundle pricing\n\n        let auction = Auction {\n            id: AuctionId::new(),\n            asset_type: AuctionAssetType::FractionBundle {\n                fraction_token_id: params.fraction_token_id,\n                amount: params.amount,\n            },\n            seller_id: params.seller_id,\n            reserve_price: params.reserve_price,\n            start_time: Utc::now(),\n            end_time: Utc::now() + params.duration,\n            status: AuctionStatus::Active,\n            highest_bid: None,\n        };\n\n        self.store.insert(auction.clone()).await?;\n        self.emit(AuctionEvent::FractionAuctionCreated(auction.id))?;\n\n        Ok(auction.id)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.5 Governance Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/governance_service/src/proposal_engine.rs`\n\n**Weighted Voting with Fractions:**\n\n```rust\nimpl<S, E, V> ProposalEngine<S, E, V>\nwhere\n    S: ProposalStore,\n    E: EventPublisher,\n    V: SignatureVerifier,\n{\n    /// Cast a vote with weight calculated from NFT + fraction holdings\n    pub async fn cast_weighted_vote(\n        &self,\n        proposal_id: Uuid,\n        voter: &str,\n        choice: VoteChoice,\n        signature: &[u8],\n    ) -> Result<(), ProposalError> {\n        // Verify signature\n        // ...\n\n        // Calculate voting weight from:\n        // 1. Whole NFT holdings\n        // 2. Fractional NFT holdings (proportional to ownership percentage)\n        let voting_weight = self.calculate_voting_power(voter).await?;\n\n        // Store vote with weight\n        self.store\n            .save_weighted_vote(proposal_id, voter, choice, voting_weight)\n            .await?;\n\n        self.events\n            .publish(GovernanceEvent::WeightedVoteCast {\n                proposal_id,\n                voter: voter.to_owned(),\n                choice,\n                weight: voting_weight,\n            })\n            .await;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate voting power including fractional ownership\n    async fn calculate_voting_power(&self, voter: &str) -> Result<u64, ProposalError> {\n        // Get whole NFT count\n        let whole_nft_power = self.get_whole_nft_count(voter).await? * 100;\n\n        // Get fractional holdings and sum weighted by ownership %\n        let fraction_holdings = self.get_fraction_holdings(voter).await?;\n        let fraction_power: u64 = fraction_holdings\n            .iter()\n            .map(|h| {\n                let ownership_pct = (h.balance as f64 / h.total_supply as f64) * 100.0;\n                ownership_pct as u64\n            })\n            .sum();\n\n        Ok(whole_nft_power + fraction_power)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Modified Outcome Calculation:**\n\n```rust\n/// Computes outcome using weighted votes\nfn compute_weighted_outcome(proposal: &Proposal, params: &GovernanceParameters) -> ProposalOutcome {\n    let total_weight: u64 = proposal.weighted_votes.values().map(|(_, w)| w).sum();\n\n    if total_weight == 0 {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_weight: u64 = proposal\n        .weighted_votes\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|(_, (choice, _))| *choice == VoteChoice::Yes)\n        .map(|(_, (_, weight))| weight)\n        .sum();\n\n    let quorum_met = total_weight >= params.required_quorum_weight;\n\n    if !quorum_met {\n        return ProposalOutcome::QuorumNotMet;\n    }\n\n    let yes_pct = (yes_weight * 100) / total_weight;\n    if yes_pct >= params.pass_threshold_pct as u64 {\n        ProposalOutcome::Accepted\n    } else {\n        ProposalOutcome::Rejected\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.6 Staking Service Changes\n\n#### File: `services/staking_service/src/staking_logic.rs`\n\n**Fraction-Aware Staking:**\n\n```rust\nimpl StakePool {\n    /// Calculate staking rewards distribution including fraction holders\n    pub async fn distribute_rewards_to_fraction_holders(\n        &self,\n        nft_id: &Uuid,\n        total_reward: u128,\n    ) -> Result<Vec<(StakerId, u128)>, StakingError> {\n        // Get all fraction holders for this NFT\n        let holders = self.get_fraction_holders(nft_id).await?;\n\n        // Calculate each holder's share proportionally\n        let distributions: Vec<(StakerId, u128)> = holders\n            .iter()\n            .map(|(staker_id, balance, total_supply)| {\n                let share = (total_reward * *balance as u128) / *total_supply as u128;\n                (staker_id.clone(), share)\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Emit distribution events\n        for (staker, amount) in &distributions {\n            self.event_tx.send(StakingEvent::FractionRewardDistributed {\n                nft_id: nft_id.to_string(),\n                staker: staker.clone(),\n                amount: *amount,\n            }).ok();\n        }\n\n        Ok(distributions)\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.7 API Gateway Changes\n\n#### File: `services/api_gateway/src/rest_api.rs`\n\n**New REST Endpoints:**\n\n```rust\npub fn payload))]\nasync fn fractionalize_nft(\n    State(state): State<AppState>,\n    Path(nft_id): Path<String>,\n    headers: HeaderMap,\n    Json(payload): Json<FractionalizeRequestBody>,\n) -> Result<impl IntoResponse, ApiError> {\n    // Validate request\n    if payload.total_fractions < 2 {\n        return Err(ApiError::BadRequest(\"must create at least 2 fractions\".into()));\n    }\n\n    // Forward to minting service via gRPC\n    let grpc_req = tonic::Request::new(proto::fractional::FractionalizeRequest {\n        nft_id,\n        owner_wallet: payload.owner_wallet,\n        total_fractions: payload.total_fractions,\n        min_trade_unit: payload.min_trade_unit.unwrap_or(1),\n        reconstitutable: payload.reconstitutable.unwrap_or(true),\n        buyout_price: payload.buyout_price,\n        signature: payload.signature,\n    });\n\n    let response = state.minting.clone()\n        .fractionalize(grpc_req)\n        .await?\n        .into_inner();\n\n    Ok((\n        StatusCode::CREATED,\n        Json(FractionalizeResponseBody {\n            fraction_token_id: response.fraction_token_id,\n            tx_hash: response.tx_hash,\n            success: response.success,\n        }),\n    ))\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"camelCase\")]\nstruct FractionalizeRequestBody {\n    pub owner_wallet: String,\n    pub total_fractions: u64,\n    pub min_trade_unit: Option<u64>,\n    pub reconstitutable: Option<bool>,\n    pub buyout_price: Option<u64>,\n    pub signature: Vec<u8>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"camelCase\")]\nstruct FractionalizeResponseBody {\n    pub fraction_token_id: String,\n    pub tx_hash: String,\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n```\n\n#### File: Core User Flows\n\n### 4.1 Flow: Owner Fractionalizing an Existing NFT\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502   Client    \u2502    \u2502  API Gateway  \u2502    \u2502 Minting Service \u2502    \u2502 Node Service \u2502    \u2502  State DB    \u2502\n\u2502   (DApp)    \u2502    \u2502  (REST API)   \u2502    \u2502    (gRPC)       \u2502    \u2502 (Consensus)  \u2502    \u2502  (sled)      \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502 1. POST /nfts/{id}/fractionalize        \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502   { totalFractions: 100, ... }          \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502 2. Validate request  \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502 3. gRPC: Fractionalize()                   \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 4. Build fractionalize tx              \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 6. Sign with service key               \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502 7. Submit tx: FractionalizeNft         \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502 8. Return response \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 16. 201 Created      \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502   { fractionTokenId, txHash }           \u2502                     \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                      \u2502                     \u2502\n```\n\n**Detailed Steps:**\n\n1. **Client Request**: User submits fractionalization request via DApp with:\n   - `nft_id`: The NFT to fractionalize\n   - `totalFractions`: Number of fractions to create (e.g., 100)\n   - `minTradeUnit`: Minimum tradeable unit (e.g., 1)\n   - `reconstitutable`: Whether NFT can be reconstituted\n   - `buyoutPrice`: Optional forced buyout price\n   - `signature`: Owner's signature authorizing the action\n\n2. **API Gateway Validation**: Validates request format, rate limits, authentication\n\n3. **gRPC Call**: Forwards to Minting Service's `Fractionalize` RPC\n\n4. **Ownership Verification**: Minting Service queries state to verify caller owns the NFT\n\n5. **Transaction Building**: Creates `FractionalizeNft` transaction payload\n\n6. **Signing**: Service signs the transaction with its operator key\n\n7. **Chain Submission**: Submits transaction to Node Service\n\n8. **Mempool Validation**: Node validates:\n   - NFT exists and is not already fractionalized\n   - Owner signature is valid\n   - Fraction count is within limits\n\n9. **Block Inclusion**: Transaction included in next block via Proof-of-Inspiration\n\n10. **State Transition**: `state_machine.rs` processes `FractionalizeNft` event\n\n11. **FractionalInfo Creation**: Creates and stores `FractionalInfo` struct attached to NFT\n\n12. **Fraction Minting**: Mints all fraction tokens to original owner's wallet\n\n13. **Event Publishing**: Publishes `nft.fractionalized` event to NATS JetStream\n\n14. **Response**: Returns transaction hash to Minting Service\n\n15. **gRPC Response**: Returns `FractionalizeResponse` to API Gateway\n\n16. **Client Response**: Returns success with `fraction_token_id` and `tx_hash`\n\n### 4.2 Flow: User Purchasing a Fraction on the Marketplace\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502   Buyer     \u2502    \u2502  API Gateway  \u2502    \u2502 Marketplace Service\u2502    \u2502 Node Service \u2502    \u2502  State DB    \u2502\n\u2502   (DApp)    \u2502    \u2502  (REST API)   \u2502    \u2502      (gRPC)        \u2502    \u2502 (Consensus)  \u2502    \u2502  (sled)      \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518     \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502 1. GET /marketplace/fractions/listings   \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502 2. gRPC: ListFractionListings()             \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500>\u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502 3. Publish events:  \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502   - FractionTransferred                 \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502   - ListingPurchased \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 15. Return result \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502<\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2502 16. 200 OK           \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502   { txHash, fractionsAcquired: 10 }      \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n       \u2502                   \u2502                       \u2502                      \u2502                   \u2502\n```\n\n**Detailed Steps:**\n\n1. **Browse Listings**: Buyer queries available fraction listings\n\n2. **gRPC Query**: API Gateway calls Marketplace Service's `ListFractionListings`\n\n3. **Database Query**: Marketplace queries listings repository\n\n4. **Return Listings**: Buyer sees available fractions with prices\n\n5. **Purchase Request**: Buyer submits purchase for 10 fractions from a listing\n\n6. **gRPC Purchase**: API Gateway calls `PurchaseFractions` RPC\n\n7. **Listing Validation**: Verify listing exists, is active, has sufficient quantity\n\n8. **Funds Validation**: Check buyer's wallet balance covers payment + gas\n\n9. **Payment Calculation**: `price_per_unit * amount = total_payment`\n\n10. **Atomic Transaction**: Create transaction with:\n    - Transfer payment from buyer to seller\n    - Transfer fractions from escrow to buyer\n    - Update or close listing\n\n11. **Transaction Validation**: Node validates all signatures and balances\n\n12. **Block Execution**: Execute atomic transfer in single block\n\n13. **State Update**: Update fraction ownership in state DB\n\n14. **Event Publishing**: Publish to NATS JetStream:\n    - `marketplace.fractions.purchased`\n    - `nft.fractions.transferred`\n\n15. **Result Return**: Return transaction result to Marketplace Service\n\n16. **Client Response**: Return success with transaction hash and acquired amount\n\n---\n\n## 5. Security Considerations\n\n### 6.1 Ownership Verification\n- All fractionalization requests must include a valid signature from the NFT owner\n- The `node_service` state machine must verify ownership before processing `FractionalizeNft` transactions\n- Double-spend protection via mempool validation (prevent racing fractionalization attempts)\n\n### 6.2 Atomic Transactions\n- All fraction transfers must be atomic (either complete fully or revert)\n- Marketplace purchases must atomically transfer both payment and fractions\n- Use database transactions in `ccs_db` to ensure consistency\n\n### 6.3 Buyout Protection\n- Implement time-locked buyout process with grace period for counter-offers\n- Require premium above market price for forced buyouts\n- Allow governance vote to block hostile buyout attempts\n\n### 6.4 Reconstitution Safeguards\n- Only allow reconstitution when holder owns exactly 100% of fractions\n- Prevent reconstitution during active auctions or pending transactions\n- Emit events for all reconstitution attempts for audit trail\n\n### 6.5 Rate Limiting\n- Apply rate limits to fractionalization requests (prevent DoS)\n- Limit number of active listings per wallet\n- Throttle fraction transfer frequency\n\n---\n\n## 7. Migration Strategy\n\n### 7.1 Database Migrations\n1. Add new columns/tables for fractional ownership tracking\n2. Deploy state_db schema changes during maintenance window\n3. Run migration scripts to index existing NFTs (mark as non-fractionalized)\n\n### 7.2 Service Deployment Order\n1. Deploy `ccs_common`, `ccs_proto`, `ccs_db` crate updates\n2. Deploy `node_service` with new transaction types (backwards compatible)\n3. Deploy `minting_service` with fractionalization endpoint\n4. Deploy `wallet_service` with fraction display support\n5. Deploy `marketplace_service` with fraction listing support\n6. Deploy `governance_service` with weighted voting\n7. Deploy `api_gateway` with new REST endpoints\n8. Enable feature flag in configuration\n\n### 7.3 Feature Flag Rollout\n- Use `[fractional_nft].enabled = false` initially\n- Enable for testnet validation\n- Gradual rollout to mainnet (canary deployment)\n- Full enablement after stability verification\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Impacted Files Summary\n\n### Critical Changes\n| File | Change Type | Priority 1. WRITE /logs/agent/solution.md
# Architectural Blueprint for Fractional NFT (F-NFT) Integration

**CanvasChain Symphony - Technical Design Document**
**Version**: 1.0.0
**Date**: 2026-02-02
**Author**: Lead Architect

---

## Executive Summary

This document provides a comprehensive architectural plan for integrating Fractional NFTs (F-NFTs) into the CanvasChain Symphony platform. The F-NFT feature will allow high-value multi-layer NFTs to be "sharded" into multiple fungible tokens, enabling fractional ownership, increased liquidity, and broader accessibility to premium digital art assets.

The design follows the existing microservices architecture using gRPC for inter-service communication and NATS JetStream for event-driven messaging, as established in ADR-001 and ADR-002.

---

## Table of Contents

1. [Impact Analysis](#1-impact-analysis)
2. [Data Model Changes](#2-data-model-changes)
3. [Component-Level Design](#3-component-level-design)
4. [Core User Flows](#4-core-user-flows)
5. [API & Configuration Changes](#5-api--configuration-changes)
6. [Security Considerations](#6-security-considerations)
7. [Migration Strategy](#7-migration-strategy)

---

## 1. Impact Analysis

### 1.1 Impacted Services

| Service | Impact Level | Description |
|---------|--------------|-------------|
| `node_service` | **Critical** | New transaction types for fractionalization and fraction transfers |
| `minting_service` | **High** | New fractionalization endpoint, fraction token creation logic |
| `wallet_service` | **High** | Display and manage fractional ownership positions |
| `marketplace_service` | **High** | List, bid, and trade fraction tokens |
| `governance_service` | **Medium** | Weighted voting based on fractional ownership |
| `staking_service` | **Medium** | Staking rewards distribution for fraction hold
... (truncated)
